### Post by danushk on 2010-02-22
Hi guys,

i need immediate help over this.

I was using Ubuntu 9.10 (Karmic Koala) , it had SDL 1.2.13 and i wanted to upgrade into SDL 1.2.14 , when i was trying to upgrade it , i was asked to use the Lucid Repositories. So i added Lucid Repositores into my apt sources list and did and upgrade , update manager went on to upgrade many packages totally around 400mb.  

After the upgrade when i restart , i can see the ubuntu karmic logo , i also hear the ubuntu login music, but i don't get the login screen. Therefore  i can't use my beloved Ubuntu !:confused:

Can somebody help me to get it working back again ? Please !

cheers

Dan

---

### Post by danushk on 2010-02-22
bump  -  Please help me !!!

---

### Post by MooPi on 2010-02-22
Can you get to recovery from boot. If you can try this;: ```
apt-get purge libsdl
```
Then : ```
apt-get install libsdl
```

---

### Post by danushk on 2010-02-23
> **MooPi said:**
> Can you get to recovery from boot. If you can try this;: ```
apt-get purge libsdl
```Then : ```
apt-get install libsdl
```

hii Moopi,

i tried but no luck.

it seems this is not an sdl related issue.  if i can remove the Lucid related upgrades , then system should work properly back again.  some Lucid updates are messing with the Gnome which could be the reason not to appear the login screen. 

How do i remove the lucid updates ?  ( i hope that would be the right step)

---

### Post by danushk on 2010-02-23
bump -  does anybody know a way to remove Lucid updates from a Karmic installation ??

---

### Post by rnerwein on 2010-02-23
hi
ok you can hear the login music, that means for me the system is ready but only the graphic don't comes up. try to get a console terminal (Ctrl + Alt + F1 (F2 ..). login as your user account and have a look at your ~/..xsession-errors ( in there i mostly found the problem when i got a problem with gnome)
ciao

have a look at /var/log/messages - kern.log - syslog - Xorg.0.log too

---

### Post by danushk on 2010-02-24
i solved the issue, 

i reinstalled Karmic , removed the SDL 1.2.13 from Synaptic and downloaded the respective packages of SDL 1.2.14 from packages.ubuntu.com , and successfully resolved the issues i had with Kdenlive screen getting chopped and scratchy sound.

yay !

---
